PREFIX bsbm: <http://www4.wiwiss.fu-berlin.de/bizer/bsbm/v01/vocabulary/> PREFIX dc: <http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/> PREFIX rev: <http://purl.org/stuff/rev#> PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/>SELECT ?title ?text ?reviewDate ?reviewer ?reviewerName ?rating1 ?rating2 ?rating3 ?rating4  WHERE {  	?review bsbm:reviewFor <http://www4.wiwiss.fu-berlin.de/bizer/bsbm/v01/instances/dataFromProducer8/Product368> . 	?review dc:title ?title . 	?review rev:text ?text . 	FILTER langMatches( lang(?text), "EN" )  	?review bsbm:reviewDate ?reviewDate . 	?review rev:reviewer ?reviewer . 	?reviewer foaf:name ?reviewerName . 	OPTIONAL { ?review bsbm:rating1 ?rating1 . } 	OPTIONAL { ?review bsbm:rating2 ?rating2 . } 	OPTIONAL { ?review bsbm:rating3 ?rating3 . } 	OPTIONAL { ?review bsbm:rating4 ?rating4 . } } ORDER BY DESC(?reviewDate) LIMIT 20
